The service was even worse. There was no welcome fruit or reception. The next day, the room was not cleaned because no one contacted me because the Do Not Disturb button was on. We stayed for two days and had to queue up for breakfast every morning. There was nothing good to eat, nor were there any Xuzhou-style snacks. Corn with black grains was placed there... Rice noodles were the most delicious, but they were basically gone if you went too late. Even the meat sauce topping was gone very quicklyüòû
We went swimming on the second night. The water in the swimming pool was quite clean, with a temperature of about 29 degrees. However, there was no swimsuit dryer or bag for wet swimsuits in the women's locker room. There was a water dispenser but no disposable paper cups. There was lotion but it was basically impossible to squeeze it out. There was a large pool of water at the entrance and exit, and it was not handled in time. I really didn't worry about guests falling...
I have stayed in so many hotels of the same price, and this was the worst one.

msg:It was my daughter's birthday and she wanted to spend New Year's Eve in a hotel, so she booked the Sheraton Hotel.
1. Location and transportation: I checked in by car. The hotel is very close to the South Third Ring Road, and the transportation is very convenient. I can reach Yunlong Lake Nanbo in a short time by car. There are large shopping malls, Mining University, Honoka Bathhouse, etc. in the surrounding area.
2. Guest rooms and facilities: The guest rooms are clean and tidy, and the basic facilities are in normal use. The decoration style of the rooms is simple and elegant, which makes people feel very comfortable. Each room has a bathtub.
3. Service quality: The hotel staff are warm, friendly and attentive. Especially the beautiful lady at the front desk, who was able to help me book a room quickly and considerate for me. Whether it is room service or catering service staff, they can provide service with a smile, making people feel extra comfortable.
4. Catering quality: The hotel's catering is rich in variety, high quality and tastes great. Breakfast and dinner can meet the needs of different guests.
5. Security: The hotel has strict security measures, which makes people feel reassured. Guest room door locks, fire protection equipment, etc. are regularly inspected.
All in all, my overall impression of this hotel is very good. The transportation is convenient, the rooms and facilities are clean and tidy, the service quality is high, the food and beverage quality is good, and safety is guaranteed. I highly recommend considering this hotel.
